(**********************************************************************************

 The displayed bicategory of two-sided displayed categories

 In this file, we define the bicategory of two-sided displayed categories. The
 displayed objects over a univalent category `C` are univalent two-sided displayed
 categories from `C` to `C`. The displayed 1-cells and 2-cells are defined
 analogously, but with functors and natural transformations instead.

 We also prove that this displayed bicategory is univalent. For that, we use the
 following idea:
 - We already know that the displayed bicategory of displayed categories is
   univalent.
 - We have an isomorphism from the displayed bicategory of two-sided displayed
   categories to the displayed bicategory of displayed categories.
 - Isomorphisms of displayed bicategories transport univalence.
 Note that this isomorphism lies over the diagonal pseudofunctor, because a
 two-sided displayed category over `C` is the same as a displayed category over
 `C × C`.

 Contents
 1. The displayed bicategory of two-sided displayed categories
 2. A pseudofunctor into displayed categories
 3. This pseudofunctor is an isomorphism
 4. The univalence
 5. Invertible 2-cells
 6. Adjoints equivalences

 **********************************************************************************)

disp_cat_ob_mor bicat_of_univ_cats


disp_cat_ob_mor bicat_of_univ_cats

  
bicat_of_univ_cats → UU
(λ obd : bicat_of_univ_cats → UU,
 ∏ x y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
 obd x → obd y → bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU)
  ?pr1

  
bicat_of_univ_cats → UU
 exact (λ (C : univalent_category), univalent_twosided_disp_cat C C).
  
(λ obd : bicat_of_univ_cats → UU,
 ∏ x y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
 obd x → obd y → bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU)
  (λ C : univalent_category,
   univalent_twosided_disp_cat C C)
 exact (λ (C₁ C₂ : univalent_category)
             (D₁ : univalent_twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₁)
             (D₂ : univalent_twosided_disp_cat C₂ C₂)
             (F : C₁ ⟶ C₂),
           twosided_disp_functor F F D₁ D₂).
Defined.

       (xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_twosided_disp_cat x),
       xx -->[ id₁ x] xx,

(λ _ : ∏ (x : bicat_of_univ_cats)
       (xx : disp_cat_ob_mor_twosided_disp_cat x),
       xx -->[ id₁ x] xx,
 ∏ (x y z : bicat_of_univ_cats)
 (f : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧)
 (g : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ y, z ⟧)

(gg2 : y -->[ g2] z),
gg1 ==>[ r] gg2 → ff ;; gg1 ==>[ f ◃ r] ff ;; gg2
 exact (λ C₁ C₂ C₃ F G₁ G₂ τ D₁ D₂ D₃ FF GG₁ GG₂ ττ,
           pre_whisker_twosided_disp_nat_trans FF ττ).

(gg : y -->[ g] z),
ff1 ==>[ r] ff2 → ff1 ;; gg ==>[ r ▹ g] ff2 ;; gg
 exact (λ C₁ C₂ C₃ F₁ F₂ G τ D₁ D₂ D₃ FF₁ FF₂ GG ττ,

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ, θ: F ==> G
p: τ = θ
D₁: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
θθ: FF ==>[ θ] GG
x, y: pr11 C₁
xy: (pr11 D₁) x y
pr1 (transportb (λ z : F ==> G, FF ==>[ z] GG) p θθ) x
  y xy = trb₂ pr1 θθ x y xy


C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ, θ: F ==> G
p: τ = θ
D₁: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
θθ: FF ==>[ θ] GG
x, y: pr11 C₁
xy: (pr11 D₁) x y
pr1 (transportb (λ z : F ==> G, FF ==>[ z] GG) p θθ) x
  y xy = trb₂ pr1 θθ x y xy

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
D₁: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
θθ: FF ==>[ τ] GG
x, y: pr11 C₁
xy: (pr11 D₁) x y
pr1
  (transportb (λ z : F ==> G, FF ==>[ z] GG)
     (idpath τ) θθ) x y xy = trb₂ pr1 θθ x y xy

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
D₁: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
θθ: FF ==>[ τ] GG
x, y: pr11 C₁
xy: (pr11 D₁) x y
pr1 θθ x y xy = pr1 θθ x y xy

  apply idpath.
Qed.


disp_prebicat_laws
  disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat


disp_prebicat_laws
  disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat

  
a, b: bicat_of_univ_cats
f, g: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ a, b ⟧
η: f ==> g
x: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat a
y: disp_prebicat_data_twosided_disp_cat b
ff: x -->[ f] y
gg: x -->[ g] y
ηη: ff ==>[ η] gg
x0, y0: a
xy: x x0 y0
id_two_disp (ff x0 y0 xy) ;;2 ηη x0 y0 xy =
trb₂ pr1 ηη x0 y0 xy
a, b: bicat_of_univ_cats
f, g: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ a, b ⟧

disp_bicat bicat_of_univ_cats


disp_bicat bicat_of_univ_cats

  
has_disp_cellset disp_prebicat_twosided_disp_cat

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
D₁: disp_prebicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_prebicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
isaset (FF ==>[ τ] GG)

  apply isaset_twosided_disp_nat_trans.
Defined.

Definition bicat_twosided_disp_cat
  : bicat
  := total_bicat disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat.

(**
 2. A pseudofunctor into displayed categories
 *)

C: category
D: twosided_disp_cat C C
disp_nat_trans
  (nat_trans_id
     (functor_identity (category_binproduct C C)))
  (disp_functor_identity
     (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat C C D))
  (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor
     (twosided_disp_functor_identity D))


C: category
D: twosided_disp_cat C C
disp_nat_trans
  (nat_trans_id
     (functor_identity (category_binproduct C C)))
  (disp_functor_identity
     (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat C C D))
  (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor
     (twosided_disp_functor_identity D))

  
C: category
D: twosided_disp_cat C C
disp_nat_trans_axioms
  (λ (x : category_binproduct C C)
   (xx : twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat C C D x),
   id_disp
     (disp_functor_identity
        (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat C C D) x xx))

  abstract
    (intros x y f xx yy ff ; cbn ;
     rewrite id_two_disp_right ;
     rewrite id_two_disp_left ;
     unfold transportb_disp_mor2, transportf_disp_mor2, transportb ;
     rewrite !twosided_prod_transport ;
     rewrite transport_f_f ;
     apply maponpaths_2 ;
     apply isasetdirprod ; apply homset_property).
Defined.


C₁, C₂, C₃: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₁
D₂: twosided_disp_cat C₂ C₂
D₃: twosided_disp_cat C₃ C₃
FF: twosided_disp_functor F F D₁ D₂
GG: twosided_disp_functor G G D₂ D₃
disp_nat_trans
  (nat_trans_id (pair_functor F F ∙ pair_functor G G))
  (disp_functor_composite
     (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor FF)
     (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor GG))
  (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor
     (comp_twosided_disp_functor FF GG))


C₁, C₂, C₃: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₁
D₂: twosided_disp_cat C₂ C₂
D₃: twosided_disp_cat C₃ C₃
FF: twosided_disp_functor F F D₁ D₂
GG: twosided_disp_functor G G D₂ D₃
disp_nat_trans
  (nat_trans_id (pair_functor F F ∙ pair_functor G G))
  (disp_functor_composite
     (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor FF)
     (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor GG))
  (two_sided_disp_functor_to_disp_functor
     (comp_twosided_disp_functor FF GG))

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₁
D₂: twosided_disp_cat C₂ C₂
D₃: twosided_disp_cat C₃ C₃
FF: twosided_disp_functor F F D₁ D₂
GG: twosided_disp_functor G G D₂ D₃

  (λ (x : category_binproduct C₁ C₁)

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
     (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lunitor diag_univ_cat F) x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
      FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ z
      ][ # F (id₁ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x))
         · id₁ (F (pr2 x))] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
         FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[
         # F (id₁ (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))
         ][ z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
        (! id_right
             (# F (id₁ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x))))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
            FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ z
            ][ # F (id₁ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x))] 
            FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
           (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr1 x))))
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
               FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[
               # F (id₁ (pr1 x))
               ][ z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
              (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr2 x))))
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
                  FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ z
                  ][ # F (id₁ (pr2 x))] FF (pr1 x)
                                          (pr2 x) xx)
                 (! functor_id F (pr1 x))
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
                     FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[
                     id₁ (F (pr1 x))
                     ][ z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
                    (! functor_id F (pr2 x))
                    (id_two_disp
                       (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))))))) =
id_two_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
     (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lunitor diag_univ_cat F) x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ _ : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
            C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
      FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ pr1 z
      ][ pr2 z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
     (pathsdirprod
        (! id_right
             (# F (id₁ (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))))
        (! id_right
             (# F (id₁ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x)))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : ∑ _ : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
               C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
         FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ pr1 z
         ][ pr2 z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
        (pathsdirprod (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr1 x))))
           (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr2 x)))))
        (transportf
           (λ z : ∑ _ : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
                  C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
            FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ pr1 z
            ][ pr2 z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
           (pathsdirprod (! functor_id F (pr1 x))
              (! functor_id F (pr2 x)))
           (id_two_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))) =
id_two_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)

    
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧

D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ _ : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,
         C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
   FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
  (pathsdirprod (! functor_id F (pr1 x))
     (! functor_id F (pr2 x)) @
   pathsdirprod (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr1 x))))
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr2 x)))) @
   pathsdirprod
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))))
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x)))) @
   nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lunitor diag_univ_cat F) x)
  (id_two_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) =
id_two_disp (FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)

     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 x), F (pr1 x) ⟧,

      ][ id₁ (F (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x))
         · id₁ (F (pr2 x))] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)
     (! id_right (id₁ (F (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F (pr2 x), F (pr2 x) ⟧,
         FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx -->[
         id₁ (F (pr1 x)) · id₁ (F (pr1 x))
         ][ z] FF (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)

             (id₁ (F (pr2 x)) · id₁ (F (pr2 x))))

     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))) =
id_two_disp
  (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))) ;;2 id_two_disp
                                         (FF₃
                                            (F₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)))
                                            (F₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x)))
                                            (FF₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x))
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x))
                                               (FF₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x) xx))) ;;2 
id_two_disp
  (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))

F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
F₃: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₄ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁

  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lassociator diag_univ_cat F₁ F₂ F₃)
     x)
  (trb₂ (id_two_disp
           (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
              (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))) ;;2 (trb₂ 
                                                 id_two_disp

                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)))

                                                 (F₁

                                                 x))
                                                 (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x))
                                                 (FF₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x) xx)))))) =
trb₂ (trb₂ id_two_disp
             (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                   (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))

    
C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧

C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
F₃: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₄ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₃
D₄: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₄
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₂ -->[ F₂] D₃
FF₃: D₃ -->[ F₃] D₄
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lassociator diag_univ_cat F₁ F₂ F₃)
     x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
            F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
      FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ z
      ][ id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
         · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
         · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))] FF₃
                                         (F₂
                                            (F₁
                                               (pr1 x)))
                                         (F₂
                                            (F₁
                                               (pr2 x)))
                                         (FF₂
                                            (F₁
                                               (pr1 x))
                                            (F₁
                                               (pr2 x))
                                            (FF₁
                                               (pr1 x)
                                               (pr2 x)
                                               xx)))
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
           · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
               F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
         FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
           (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
              (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
         id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
         · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
         ][ z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                 (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                    (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
        (! id_right
             (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
              · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                  F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
            FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
              (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ z
            ][ id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
               · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))] FF₃
                                                 (F₂
                                                 (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)))
                                                 (F₂
                                                 (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x)))
                                                 (FF₂
                                                 (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x))
                                                 (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x))
                                                 (FF₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x) xx)))
           (! id_left (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
                     F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
               FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                 (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                    (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
               # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
               ][ z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                       (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                       (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                          (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
              (! id_left
                   (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))))
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                        F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
                  FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                    (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                    (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                       (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
                  z
                  ][ # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))] 
                  FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                    (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                    (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                       (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
                 (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
                           F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
                     FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                       (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                       (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                          (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
                     id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
                     ][ z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                             (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                             (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))
                                (F₁ (pr2 x))
                                (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)
                                   xx)))
                    (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
                    (id_two_disp
                       (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                          (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                          (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))
                             (F₁ (pr2 x))
                             (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))))))))) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
         F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
   FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ z
   ][ id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
      · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
      · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))] FF₃
                                      (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                                      (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                                      (FF₂
                                         (F₁ (pr1 x))
                                         (F₁ (pr2 x))
                                         (FF₁ (pr1 x)
                                            (pr2 x) xx)))
  (! id_right
       (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
        · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
            F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
      FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
      id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
      · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
      ][ z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
              (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
           · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
               F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
         FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
           (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
              (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ z
         ][ id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
            · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))] FF₃
                                            (F₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)))
                                            (F₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x)))
                                            (FF₂
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x))
                                               (F₁
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x))
                                               (FF₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x) xx)))
        (! id_right (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
                  F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
            FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
              (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[
            id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
            ][ z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                    (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                    (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                       (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
           (! id_right (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))))
           (id_two_disp
              (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                 (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                    (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))))))

    
C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
F₃: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₃, C₄ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₃
D₄: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₄
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₂ -->[ F₂] D₃
FF₃: D₃ -->[ F₃] D₄
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lassociator diag_univ_cat F₁ F₂ F₃)
     x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑
            _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
            C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
            F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
      FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
      ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                  (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                  (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (pathsdirprod
        (! id_right
             (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
              · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
        (! id_right
             (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
              · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : ∑
               _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                   F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
               C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
               F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
         FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
           (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
              (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
         ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                     (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
        (pathsdirprod
           (! id_left (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
           (! id_left (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))))
        (transportf
           (λ z : ∑
                  _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                      F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
                  C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
                  F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
            FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
              (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
            ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                        (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
           (pathsdirprod
              (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
              (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))
           (id_two_disp
              (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                 (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                    (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))))))) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑
         _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
             F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
         C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
         F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
   FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
               (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                  (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
  (pathsdirprod
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
           · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
           · id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑
            _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
                F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
            C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
            F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
      FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
      ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)))
                  (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
                  (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
     (pathsdirprod
        (! id_right (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
        (! id_right (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))))
     (id_two_disp
        (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
           (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
              (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))))

    
C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧

  D₁ x
transportf
  (λ z : ∑
         _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
             F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
         C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
         F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,
   FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
     (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
               (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                  (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
  (pathsdirprod (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
     (! functor_id F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))) @
   pathsdirprod
     (! id_left (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
     (! id_left (# F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))) @
   pathsdirprod
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))
           · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))
     (! id_right
          (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))))
           · # F₃ (id₁ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))))) @
   nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_lassociator diag_univ_cat F₁ F₂ F₃)
     x)
  (id_two_disp
     (FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
        (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑
         _ : C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))),
             F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) ⟧,
         C₄ ⟦ F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))),
         F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x))) ⟧,

   ][ pr2 z] FF₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))) (F₂ (F₁ (pr2 x)))
               (FF₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
                  (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
  (pathsdirprod
     (! id_right (id₁ (F₃ (F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x))))))

C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
D₃: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₃

GG: D₂ -->[ G] D₃
ττ: FF₁ ==>[ τ] FF₂
x: diag_univ_cat C₁
xx: twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor_data C₁
  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
     (GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
        (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_rwhisker diag_univ_cat G τ) x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
      GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ z
      ][ # G (τ (pr2 x)) · id₁ (G (F₂ (pr2 x)))] GG
                                                 (F₂
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x))
                                                 (F₂
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x))
                                                 (FF₂
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 x) xx))
     (! id_right (# G (τ (pr1 x))))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
         GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
           (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[
         # G (τ (pr1 x))
         ][ z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
                 (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
        (! id_right (# G (τ (pr2 x))))
        ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
   GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ z
   ][ id₁ (G (F₁ (pr2 x))) · # (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr2 x))] 
   GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
     (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr1 x))))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
      GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[
      # (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr1 x))
      ][ z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
              (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
     (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr2 x))))
     ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))

    
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂

  D₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
     (GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
        (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_rwhisker diag_univ_cat G τ) x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑
            _ : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
            C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
      GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
        (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ pr1 z
      ][ pr2 z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
                  (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
     (pathsdirprod (! id_right (# G (τ (pr1 x))))
        (! id_right (# G (τ (pr2 x)))))
     ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ _ : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
         C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
   GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
               (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (pathsdirprod
     (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr1 x))))
     (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr2 x)))))
  ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))

τ: F₁ ==> F₂

  D₁ x
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ _ : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
         C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
   GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
               (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (pathsdirprod (! id_right (# G (τ (pr1 x))))
     (! id_right (# G (τ (pr2 x)))) @
   nat_trans_eq_pointwise
     (! psfunctor_rwhisker diag_univ_cat G τ) x)
  ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx)) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ _ : C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr1 x)), G (F₂ (pr1 x)) ⟧,
         C₃ ⟦ G (F₁ (pr2 x)), G (F₂ (pr2 x)) ⟧,
   GG (F₁ (pr1 x)) (F₁ (pr2 x))
     (FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx) -->[ pr1 z
   ][ pr2 z] GG (F₂ (pr1 x)) (F₂ (pr2 x))
               (FF₂ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))
  (pathsdirprod
     (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr1 x))))
     (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr2 x)))))
  ((#2 GG) (ττ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) xx))

F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁

  D₁ x
pathsdirprod (! id_right (# G (τ (pr1 x))))
  (! id_right (# G (τ (pr2 x)))) @
nat_trans_eq_pointwise
  (! psfunctor_rwhisker diag_univ_cat G τ) x =
pathsdirprod (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr1 x))))
  (! id_left (# (pr1 G) (pr1 τ (pr2 x))))

    apply isasetdirprod ; apply homset_property.
Qed.

(**
 3. This pseudofunctor is an isomorphism
 *)

disp_psfunctor_iso
  twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor


disp_psfunctor_iso
  twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor

  
∏ x : bicat_of_univ_cats,
isweq (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor x)
∏ (x y : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(f : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(xx : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat x)
(yy : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat y),
isweq
  (λ ff : xx -->[ f] yy,
   ♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ff)
∏ (x y : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(f g : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧) (τ : f ==> g)
(xx : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat x)
(yy : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat y)
(ff : xx -->[ f] yy) (gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
isweq
  (λ ττ : ff ==>[ τ] gg,
   ♯♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ττ)

  
∏ x : bicat_of_univ_cats,
isweq (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor x)
 
C: bicat_of_univ_cats
isweq (twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor C)

    exact (pr2 (univalent_twosided_disp_cat_weq_univalent_disp_cat _ _)).
  
∏ (x y : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(f : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(xx : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat x)
(yy : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat y),
isweq
  (λ ff : xx -->[ f] yy,
   ♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ff)
 
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
isweq
  (λ ff : D₁ -->[ F] D₂,
   ♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ff)

    exact (pr2 (two_sided_disp_functor_weq_disp_functor F F (pr1 D₁) (pr1 D₂))).
  
∏ (x y : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(f g : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ x, y ⟧) (τ : f ==> g)
(xx : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat x)
(yy : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat y)
(ff : xx -->[ f] yy) (gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
isweq
  (λ ττ : ff ==>[ τ] gg,
   ♯♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ττ)
 
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
isweq
  (λ ττ : FF ==>[ τ] GG,
   ♯♯ twosided_disp_cat_to_disp_cat_psfunctor ττ)

    exact (pr2 (twosided_disp_nat_trans_weq_disp_nat_trans τ τ FF GG)).
Defined.

(**
 5. Invertible 2-cells
 *)
Section ToInvertible.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : univalent_category}
          {F : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
          {D₁ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁}
          {D₂ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂}
          {FF GG : D₁ -->[ F ] D₂}
          (ττ : FF ==>[ id2 _ ] GG)
          (Hττ : ∏ (x y : C₁)
                   (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
                 is_iso_twosided_disp
                   (identity_is_z_iso _)
                   (identity_is_z_iso _)
                   (pr1 ττ x y f)).

  Definition is_disp_invertible_2cell_twosided_disp_cat_over_id_inv_data
    : twosided_disp_nat_trans_data
        (nat_trans_id _) (nat_trans_id _)
        (pr1 GG)
        (pr1 FF)
    := λ x y f, iso_inv_twosided_disp (Hττ x y f).

  Arguments is_disp_invertible_2cell_twosided_disp_cat_over_id_inv_data /.

  
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))
(pr1 ττ x y f)
twosided_disp_nat_trans_laws (nat_trans_id F)
  (nat_trans_id F) (pr1 GG) (pr1 FF)
  is_disp_invertible_2cell_twosided_disp_cat_over_id_inv_data

  
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))
(pr1 ττ x y f)
twosided_disp_nat_trans_laws (nat_trans_id F)
  (nat_trans_id F) (pr1 GG) (pr1 FF)
  is_disp_invertible_2cell_twosided_disp_cat_over_id_inv_data

    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))
(pr1 ττ x y f)
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: D₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: D₁ x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
(#2 (pr1 GG)) fg ;;2 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                       (Hττ x₂ y₂ xy₂) =
trb₂ (iso_inv_twosided_disp (Hττ x₁ y₁ xy₁) ;;2 (#2 
                                                 (pr1
                                                 FF))
                                                 fg)

    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))

g: C₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: D₁ x₁ y₁

fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂

                                                 fg) =
(#2 (pr1 GG)) fg ;;2 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                       (Hττ x₂ y₂ xy₂)

?b
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),

?b =
(#2 (pr1 GG)) fg ;;2 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                       (Hττ x₂ y₂ xy₂)

    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))
(pr1 ττ x y f)
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: D₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: D₁ x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
trf₂ (iso_inv_twosided_disp (Hττ x₁ y₁ xy₁) ;;2 ((#2 
                                                 (pr1
                                                 FF))
                                                 fg ;;2 
                                                 (pr1
                                                 ττ x₂
                                                 y₂
                                                 xy₂ ;;2 
                                                 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                                                 (Hττ
                                                 x₂ y₂
                                                 xy₂)))) =
?b

(#2 (pr1 FF)) fg ;;2 (pr1 ττ x₂ y₂ xy₂ ;;2 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                                             (Hττ x₂
                                                y₂ xy₂)) =
?t2

FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso (F x)) (identity_is_z_iso (F y))
(pr1 ττ x y f)
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: D₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: D₁ x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
trf₂ (iso_inv_twosided_disp (Hττ x₁ y₁ xy₁) ;;2 pr1 ττ
                                                 x₁ y₁
                                                 xy₁ ;;2 
      (#2 (pr1 GG)) fg ;;2 iso_inv_twosided_disp
                             (Hττ x₂ y₂ xy₂)) = ?b

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: invertible_2cell F G
Hτ:= is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)
  (pr2 τ): is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ τ] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr1 C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f)

  (is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ) Hτ) ττ


C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: invertible_2cell F G
Hτ:= is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)
  (pr2 τ): is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ τ] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr1 C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f)
is_disp_invertible_2cell
  (is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ) Hτ) ττ

  
∏ (C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(F G : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧)
(τ : invertible_2cell F G)
(Hτ :=
 is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ) (pr2 τ))
(D₁ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁)
(D₂ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂)
(FF : D₁ -->[ F] D₂) (GG : D₁ -->[ G] D₂)
(ττ : FF ==>[ τ] GG),
(∏ (x y : pr1 C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
 is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f))
→ is_disp_invertible_2cell
    (is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ) Hτ)
    ττ

  
is_univalent_2_1 bicat_of_univ_cats
∏ (a b : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(f : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ a, b ⟧),
(λ (a0 b0 : bicat_of_univ_cats)
 (f0 g : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧)
 (α : invertible_2cell f0 g),
 ∏
 (Hτ :=
  is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso (pr1 α) (pr2 α))
 (D₁ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat a0)
 (D₂ : disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat b0)
 (FF : D₁ -->[ f0] D₂) (GG : D₁ -->[ g] D₂)
 (ττ : FF ==>[ α] GG),
 (∏ (x y : pr1 a0) (f1 : pr1 D₁ x y),
  is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f1))
 → is_disp_invertible_2cell
     (is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell (pr1 α) Hτ)
     ττ) a b f f (id2_invertible_2cell f)

  
is_univalent_2_1 bicat_of_univ_cats
 exact univalent_cat_is_univalent_2_1.

τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
GG: D₁ -->[ G] D₂
ττ: FF ==>[ τ] GG
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr1 C₁) (f : pr1 D₁ x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f)
x, y: pr1 C₁
f: pr1 D₁ x y
is_iso_twosided_disp
  (is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso
     (pr1
        (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
     (pr2
        (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
     x)
  (is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso
     (pr1
        (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
     (pr2
        (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
     y) (pr1 ττ x y f)

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂

  x

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)
D₁: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_twosided_disp_cat C₂

is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f)
x, y: pr1 C₁
f: pr1 D₁ x y
Hτ x =
is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso
  (pr1 (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
  (pr2 (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
  x
 apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr1 τ)

is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) (pr1 ττ x y f)

f: pr1 D₁ x y
Hτ y =
is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso
  (pr1 (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
  (pr2 (τ,, is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell τ Hτ))
  y
 apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
Qed.

τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
is_invertible_2cell τ

is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
is_invertible_2cell τ

  
CD₁, CD₂: bicat_twosided_disp_cat

τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
∑ Hα : is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ),
is_disp_invertible_2cell Hα (pr2 τ)

τ: F ==> G

Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),

 is_disp_invertible_2cell Hα (pr2 τ)) ?pr1

Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)

is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ)
 
CD₁, CD₂: bicat_twosided_disp_cat
F, G: bicat_twosided_disp_cat ⟦ CD₁, CD₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)

    exact Hτ.
  
CD₁, CD₂: bicat_twosided_disp_cat
F, G: bicat_twosided_disp_cat ⟦ CD₁, CD₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
(λ Hα : is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ),
 is_disp_invertible_2cell Hα (pr2 τ))
  (is_nat_z_iso_to_is_invertible_2cell (pr1 τ) Hτ)
 
CD₁, CD₂: bicat_twosided_disp_cat
F, G: bicat_twosided_disp_cat ⟦ CD₁, CD₂ ⟧
τ: F ==> G
Hτ: is_nat_z_iso (pr11 τ)
Hττ: ∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)
∏ (x y : pr11 CD₁) (f : (pr12 CD₁) x y),
is_iso_twosided_disp (Hτ x) (Hτ y) ((pr12 τ) x y f)

    exact Hττ.
Qed.
